張愛(angry): 媽！怎麼能這樣呢？
Mom, how could this happen?

宋喬(disgust): 她說得不對啊？離婚協議書沒起效，她們現在還算是夫妻，我能有什麼辦法？要不，你去找開鎖工，逼着她跳樓？我不管了，我這一天都累死了，我要去睡了，你們這事我也管不了。
She's not right. The divorce papers don't work. They're still married. What can I do?

張愛: 媽，我去找開鎖工吧？
張心: 有本事你找去！你要是敢找，我就敢從窗戶跳下去信不信？我說到做到！有本事你找去吧！
張愛: 張心你還講不講理啊？
張心: 我怎麼不講理了？啊？我讓我自己的老公回自己的房間睡覺，這有什麼不對的？還是我這樣做犯了什麼法了？啊？

What is the emotion of 宋喬 here?
The emotion of 宋喬 here is anger.
Is 張愛 the primary reason for 宋喬 feeling anger?
Yes, 張愛 is the primary reason for 宋喬 feeling anger. 張愛 is not following 宋喬's instructions to go back to her room and sleep, which is causing 宋喬 to be angry.
Did 張愛 violate any social norm? If so, which norm?
Yes, 張愛 violated the social norm of respecting one's elders. 張愛 should have listened to 宋喬 and gone back to her room to sleep instead of arguing with her.
How exactly did 張愛 made 宋喬 feel anger?
張愛 made 宋喬 feel anger by arguing with her and not following her instructions.

1246
張心(neutral): 爸。
Dad.

宋喬(disgust): 你就別再煩他了，他現在啊已經夠氣的了！
Don't bother him anymore. He's mad enough now!

張心(fear): 爸的手怎麼樣了？
How's Dad's hand?

宋喬(angry): 還好意思問！幸虧及時處理了傷口，醫生說沒什麼大礙。你怎麼可以咬你爸爸呢？
I'm glad you took care of the wound in time. The doctor said it's no big deal. How can you bite your father?

張心(fear): 我也是急得沒辦法了嘛！
I can't help myself!

宋喬(angry): 再怎麼說他也是你爸爸，再沒辦法也不能咬他啊？
He's your father anyway. You can't bite him anymore?

張心(fear): 我錯了！我知道錯了！真的！媽，你替我勸勸爸吧！
I'm wrong! I know I'm wrong! Really, Mom, please talk to Dad for me!

宋喬(surprise): 我怎麼勸啊？
How am I supposed to do that?

張心(fear): 你真想看到我和爸整天這樣啊？
You really want to see me and Dad do this all day?

宋喬(angry): 現在他哪有心思跟你計較？他現在正在擔心你姐呢！想讓他原諒，你就保佑你姐沒事吧！記住了，千萬別在惹他生氣了！不然，我也不管你了！
What's he thinking about now? He's worried about your sister. If you want him to forgive you, you'll keep your sister safe. Remember, don't get mad at him. Otherwise, I don't care about you.

張心(fear): 是。我知道。我一定好好聽話。不惹你們生氣。
Yeah, I know. I'm gonna be good. I'm not gonna piss you off.
